MRC_civil_war_scripted_effects_for_original = {
	delete_unit_template_and_units = {
		division_template = "Military Militia"
		disband = yes # if yes, will refund equipment/manpower.
	}

	division_template = {
	    name = "Military Militia"
	    is_locked = yes
	    #division_names_group = GER_INF_01
	    priority = 0
	    template_counter = 42 # The Viking Helmet 
	    regiments = {
	        militia = { x = 0 y = 0 }
	        militia = { x = 0 y = 1 }
	        militia = { x = 0 y = 2 }
	        militia = { x = 0 y = 3 }
	    }
	}

	random_state = {
		limit = {
			is_in_home_area = yes
			is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
		}
		create_unit = {
		    division = "name = \"Military Militia\" division_template = \"Military Militia\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 0.7"
		    owner = ROOT
		}
		create_unit = {
		    division = "name = \"Military Militia\" division_template = \"Military Militia\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 0.7"
		    owner = ROOT
		}

MRC_civil_war_scripted_effects_for_semidemocracy = {
	PREV = { # Original country
		MRC_lucius_iuvenum = { # Character
		    set_nationality = PREV.PREV
		    # Transfers to breakaway
		}
		MRC_philip_flavius = { # Character
		    set_nationality = PREV.PREV
		    # Transfers to breakaway
		}
		MRC_marcus_commercium = { # Character
		    set_nationality = PREV.PREV
		    # Transfers to breakaway
		}
		MRC_gracia_fidaelis = { # Character
		    set_nationality = PREV.PREV
		    # Transfers to breakaway
		}
	}

	IF = {
		limit = {
			PREV.PREV = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_leader = {
						ruling_only = yes
						character = MRC_gracia_fidaelis
					}
				}
				has_civil_war = yes
			}
		}
		PREV.PREV = {
			MRC_gracia_fidaelis = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = sub_mercantile_republicism
						traits = { trait_species_human hero_from_the_independence_era_young }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

    PREV.PREV = {
		delete_unit_template_and_units = {
			division_template = "Military Militia"
			disband = yes # if yes, will refund equipment/manpower.
		}

		division_template = {
		    name = "Military Militia"
		    is_locked = yes
		    #division_names_group = GER_INF_01
		    priority = 0
		    template_counter = 42 # The Viking Helmet 
		    regiments = {
		        militia = { x = 0 y = 0 }
		        militia = { x = 0 y = 1 }
		        militia = { x = 0 y = 2 }
		        militia = { x = 0 y = 3 }
		    }
		}
		random_state = {
			limit = {
				is_in_home_area = yes
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = PREV
			}
			create_unit = {
			    division = "name = \"Military Militia\" division_template = \"Military Militia\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 0.7"
			    owner = PREV 
			}
			create_unit = {
			    division = "name = \"Military Militia\" division_template = \"Military Militia\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 0.7"
			    owner = PREV 
			}
			create_unit = {
			    division = "name = \"Military Militia\" division_template = \"Military Militia\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 0.7"
			    owner = PREV 
			}
			create_unit = {
			    division = "name = \"Military Militia\" division_template = \"Military Militia\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 0.7"
			    owner = PREV 
			}
			create_unit = {
			    division = "name = \"Military Militia\" division_template = \"Military Militia\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 0.7"
			    owner = PREV 
			}
			create_unit = {
			    division = "name = \"Military Militia\" division_template = \"Military Militia\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 0.7"
			    owner = PREV 
			}
			create_unit = {
			    division = "name = \"Military Militia\" division_template = \"Military Militia\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 0.7"
			    owner = PREV 
			}
			create_unit = {
			    division = "name = \"Military Militia\" division_template = \"Military Militia\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 0.7"

MRC_theocratism_civil_war_scripted_effects_for_semidemocracy = {
	MRC_civil_war_scripted_effects_for_semidemocracy = yes
}

MRC_unitism_civil_war_scripted_effects_for_semidemocracy = {
	MRC_civil_war_scripted_effects_for_semidemocracy = yes
}

MRC_amc_primary_champion_star_add = {
	IF = {
		LIMIT = { check_variable = { MRC_amc_primary_champion_star < 6.5 } }
		add_to_variable = {
			var = MRC_amc_primary_champion_star
			value = 1
			tooltip = MRC_primary_airframe_improve_tt
		}
		clamp_temp_variable = {
			var = MRC_amc_primary_champion_star
			min = 0
			max = 7
		}
	}
}

MRC_amc_secondary_champion_star_add = {
	IF = {
		LIMIT = { check_variable = { MRC_amc_secondary_champion_star < 4.5 } }
		add_to_variable = {
			var = MRC_amc_secondary_champion_star
			value = 1
			tooltip = MRC_secondary_airframe_improve_tt
		}
		clamp_temp_variable = {
			var = MRC_amc_secondary_champion_star
			min = 0
			max = 5
		}
	}
}

MRC_amc_trinary_champion_star_add = {
	IF = {
		LIMIT = { check_variable = { MRC_amc_trinary_champion_star < 2.5 } }
		add_to_variable = {
			var = MRC_amc_trinary_champion_star
			value = 1
			tooltip = MRC_trinary_airframe_improve_tt
		}
		clamp_temp_variable = {
			var = MRC_amc_trinary_champion_star
			min = 0
			max = 3
		}
	}
}

MRC_amc_primary_champion_star_remove = {
	IF = {
		LIMIT = { check_variable = { MRC_amc_primary_champion_star < 6.5 } }
		subtract_from_variable = {
			var = MRC_amc_primary_champion_star
			value = 1
			tooltip = MRC_primary_airframe_worsen_tt
		}
		clamp_temp_variable = {
			var = MRC_amc_primary_champion_star
			min = 0
			max = 7
		}
	}
}

MRC_amc_secondary_champion_star_remove = {
	IF = {
		LIMIT = { check_variable = { MRC_amc_secondary_champion_star < 4.5 } }
		subtract_from_variable = {
			var = MRC_amc_secondary_champion_star
			value = 1
			tooltip = MRC_secondary_airframe_worsen_tt
		}
		clamp_temp_variable = {
			var = MRC_amc_secondary_champion_star
			min = 0
			max = 5
		}
	}
}

MRC_amc_trinary_champion_star_remove = {
	IF = {
		LIMIT = { check_variable = { MRC_amc_trinary_champion_star < 2.5 } }
		subtract_from_variable = {
			var = MRC_amc_trinary_champion_star
			value = 1
			tooltip = MRC_trinary_airframe_worsen_tt
		}
		clamp_temp_variable = {
			var = MRC_amc_trinary_champion_star
			min = 0
			max = 3
		}
	}
}

MRC_idea_small_plane_airframe_build_cost_ic_num_ns = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = modify_MRC_idea_air_manufacturing_modifier_tt
	custom_effect_tooltip = MRC_small_plane_airframe_modify_tt
	#custom_effect_tooltip = MRC_military_small_plane_airframe_build_cost_ic_0_key
	hidden_effect = {
		IF = {
			LIMIT = {
				NOT = {
					has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_build_cost_ic_0_ns
					has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_build_cost_ic_1_ns
					has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_build_cost_ic_2_ns
					has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_build_cost_ic_3_ns
					has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_build_cost_ic_4_ns
				}
			}
			add_ideas = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_build_cost_ic_0_ns
		}
		ELSE_IF = {
			LIMIT = { has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_build_cost_ic_0_ns }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_build_cost_ic_0_ns
				add_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_build_cost_ic_1_ns
			}
		}
		ELSE_IF = {
			LIMIT = { has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_build_cost_ic_1_ns }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_build_cost_ic_1_ns
				add_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_build_cost_ic_2_ns
			}
		}
		ELSE_IF = {
			LIMIT = { has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_build_cost_ic_2_ns }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_build_cost_ic_2_ns
				add_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_build_cost_ic_3_ns
			}
		}
		ELSE_IF = {
			LIMIT = { has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_build_cost_ic_3_ns }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_build_cost_ic_3_ns
				add_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_build_cost_ic_4_ns
			}
		}
	}
}

MRC_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_attack_num_ns = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = modify_MRC_idea_air_manufacturing_modifier_tt
	custom_effect_tooltip = MRC_small_plane_airframe_modify_tt
	#custom_effect_tooltip = MRC_military_small_plane_airframe_air_attack_0_key
	hidden_effect = {
		IF = {
			LIMIT = {
				NOT = {
					has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_attack_0_ns
					has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_attack_1_ns
					has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_attack_2_ns
					has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_attack_3_ns
					has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_attack_4_ns
				}
			}
			add_ideas = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_attack_0_ns
		}
		ELSE_IF = {
			LIMIT = { has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_attack_0_ns }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_attack_0_ns
				add_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_attack_1_ns
			}
		}
		ELSE_IF = {
			LIMIT = { has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_attack_1_ns }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_attack_1_ns
				add_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_attack_2_ns
			}
		}
		ELSE_IF = {
			LIMIT = { has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_attack_2_ns }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_attack_2_ns
				add_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_attack_3_ns
			}
		}
		ELSE_IF = {
			LIMIT = { has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_attack_3_ns }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_attack_3_ns
				add_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_attack_4_ns
			}
		}
	}
}

MRC_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_defence_num_ns = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = modify_MRC_idea_air_manufacturing_modifier_tt
	custom_effect_tooltip = MRC_small_plane_airframe_modify_tt
	#custom_effect_tooltip = MRC_military_small_plane_airframe_air_defence_0_key
	hidden_effect = {
		IF = {
			LIMIT = {
				NOT = {
					has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_defence_0_ns
					has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_defence_1_ns
					has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_defence_2_ns
					has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_defence_3_ns
					has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_defence_4_ns
				}
			}
			add_ideas = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_defence_0_ns
		}
		ELSE_IF = {
			LIMIT = { has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_defence_0_ns }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_defence_0_ns
				add_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_defence_1_ns
			}
		}
		ELSE_IF = {
			LIMIT = { has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_defence_1_ns }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_defence_1_ns
				add_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_defence_2_ns
			}
		}
		ELSE_IF = {
			LIMIT = { has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_defence_2_ns }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_defence_2_ns
				add_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_defence_3_ns
			}
		}
		ELSE_IF = {
			LIMIT = { has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_defence_3_ns }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_defence_3_ns
				add_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_defence_4_ns
			}
		}
	}

MRC_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_range_num_ns = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = modify_MRC_idea_air_manufacturing_modifier_tt
	custom_effect_tooltip = MRC_small_plane_airframe_modify_tt
	#custom_effect_tooltip = MRC_military_small_plane_airframe_air_range_0_key
	hidden_effect = {
		IF = {
			LIMIT = {
				NOT = {
					has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_range_0_ns
					has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_range_1_ns
					has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_range_2_ns
					has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_range_3_ns
					has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_range_4_ns
				}
			}
			add_ideas = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_range_0_ns
		}
		ELSE_IF = {
			LIMIT = { has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_range_0_ns }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_range_0_ns
				add_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_range_1_ns
			}
		}
		ELSE_IF = {
			LIMIT = { has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_range_1_ns }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_range_1_ns
				add_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_range_2_ns
			}
		}
		ELSE_IF = {
			LIMIT = { has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_range_2_ns }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_range_2_ns
				add_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_range_3_ns
			}
		}
		ELSE_IF = {
			LIMIT = { has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_range_3_ns }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_range_3_ns
				add_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_range_4_ns
			}
		}
	}
}

MRC_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_agility_num_ns = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = modify_MRC_idea_air_manufacturing_modifier_tt
	custom_effect_tooltip = MRC_small_plane_airframe_modify_tt
	#custom_effect_tooltip = MRC_military_small_plane_airframe_air_agility_0_key
	hidden_effect = {
		IF = {
			LIMIT = {
				NOT = {
					has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_agility_0_ns
					has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_agility_1_ns
					has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_agility_2_ns
					has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_agility_3_ns
					has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_agility_4_ns
				}
			}
			add_ideas = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_agility_0_ns
		}
		ELSE_IF = {
			LIMIT = { has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_agility_0_ns }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_agility_0_ns
				add_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_agility_1_ns
			}
		}
		ELSE_IF = {
			LIMIT = { has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_agility_1_ns }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_agility_1_ns
				add_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_agility_2_ns
			}
		}
		ELSE_IF = {
			LIMIT = { has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_agility_2_ns }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_agility_2_ns
				add_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_agility_3_ns
			}
		}
		ELSE_IF = {
			LIMIT = { has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_agility_3_ns }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_agility_3_ns
				add_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_agility_4_ns
			}
		}
	}
}

MRC_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_ground_attack_num_ns = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = modify_MRC_idea_air_manufacturing_modifier_tt
	custom_effect_tooltip = MRC_small_plane_airframe_modify_tt
	#custom_effect_tooltip = MRC_military_small_plane_airframe_air_ground_attack_0_key
	hidden_effect = {
		IF = {
			LIMIT = {
				NOT = {
					has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_ground_attack_0_ns
					has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_ground_attack_1_ns
					has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_ground_attack_2_ns
					has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_ground_attack_3_ns
					has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_ground_attack_4_ns
				}
			}
			add_ideas = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_ground_attack_0_ns
		}
		ELSE_IF = {
			LIMIT = { has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_ground_attack_0_ns }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_ground_attack_0_ns
				add_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_ground_attack_1_ns
			}
		}
		ELSE_IF = {
			LIMIT = { has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_ground_attack_1_ns }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_ground_attack_1_ns
				add_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_ground_attack_2_ns
			}
		}
		ELSE_IF = {
			LIMIT = { has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_ground_attack_2_ns }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_ground_attack_2_ns
				add_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_ground_attack_3_ns
			}
		}
		ELSE_IF = {
			LIMIT = { has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_ground_attack_3_ns }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_ground_attack_3_ns
				add_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_small_plane_airframe_air_ground_attack_4_ns
			}
		}
	}
}

	custom_effect_tooltip = MRC_cv_small_plane_naval_bomber_airframe_modify_tt
	#custom_effect_tooltip = MRC_military_cv_small_plane_naval_bomber_airframe_air_ground_attack_0_key
	hidden_effect = {
		IF = {
			LIMIT = {
				NOT = {
					has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_cv_small_plane_naval_bomber_airframe_air_ground_attack_0_ns
					has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_cv_small_plane_naval_bomber_airframe_air_ground_attack_1_ns
					has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_cv_small_plane_naval_bomber_airframe_air_ground_attack_2_ns
					has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_cv_small_plane_naval_bomber_airframe_air_ground_attack_3_ns
					has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_cv_small_plane_naval_bomber_airframe_air_ground_attack_4_ns
				}
			}
			add_ideas = MRC_hidden_idea_cv_small_plane_naval_bomber_airframe_air_ground_attack_0_ns
		}
		ELSE_IF = {
			LIMIT = { has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_cv_small_plane_naval_bomber_airframe_air_ground_attack_0_ns }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_cv_small_plane_naval_bomber_airframe_air_ground_attack_0_ns
				add_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_cv_small_plane_naval_bomber_airframe_air_ground_attack_1_ns
			}
		}
		ELSE_IF = {
			LIMIT = { has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_cv_small_plane_naval_bomber_airframe_air_ground_attack_1_ns }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_cv_small_plane_naval_bomber_airframe_air_ground_attack_1_ns
				add_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_cv_small_plane_naval_bomber_airframe_air_ground_attack_2_ns
			}
		}
		ELSE_IF = {
			LIMIT = { has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_cv_small_plane_naval_bomber_airframe_air_ground_attack_2_ns }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_cv_small_plane_naval_bomber_airframe_air_ground_attack_2_ns
				add_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_cv_small_plane_naval_bomber_airframe_air_ground_attack_3_ns
			}
		}
		ELSE_IF = {
			LIMIT = { has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_cv_small_plane_naval_bomber_airframe_air_ground_attack_3_ns }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_cv_small_plane_naval_bomber_airframe_air_ground_attack_3_ns
				add_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_cv_small_plane_naval_bomber_airframe_air_ground_attack_4_ns
			}
		}
	}

MRC_idea_carrier_build_cost_ic_num_ns = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = modify_MRC_idea_navy_manufacturing_modifier_tt
	#custom_effect_tooltip = MRC_military_carrier_build_cost_ic_0_key
	hidden_effect = {
		IF = {
			LIMIT = {
				NOT = {
					has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_carrier_build_cost_ic_0_ns
					has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_carrier_build_cost_ic_1_ns
					has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_carrier_build_cost_ic_2_ns
					has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_carrier_build_cost_ic_3_ns
					has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_carrier_build_cost_ic_4_ns
				}
			}
			add_ideas = MRC_hidden_idea_carrier_build_cost_ic_0_ns
		}
		ELSE_IF = {
			LIMIT = { has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_carrier_build_cost_ic_0_ns }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_carrier_build_cost_ic_0_ns
				add_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_carrier_build_cost_ic_1_ns
			}
		}
		ELSE_IF = {
			LIMIT = { has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_carrier_build_cost_ic_1_ns }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_carrier_build_cost_ic_1_ns
				add_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_carrier_build_cost_ic_2_ns
			}
		}
		ELSE_IF = {
			LIMIT = { has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_carrier_build_cost_ic_2_ns }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_carrier_build_cost_ic_2_ns
				add_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_carrier_build_cost_ic_3_ns
			}
		}
		ELSE_IF = {
			LIMIT = { has_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_carrier_build_cost_ic_3_ns }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_carrier_build_cost_ic_3_ns
				add_idea = MRC_hidden_idea_carrier_build_cost_ic_4_ns
			}
		}
	}
}
